The actual area of â€‹â€‹the room is much smaller than that introduced in Ctrip's advertisement, and even the picture of the luxury standard room was used instead of the introduction of the business standard room, which failed to operate with integrity. After negotiating with the front desk several times at night, I was exempted from upgrading. The waiter in the room depar**ent has a good attitude. I ran a few times to deliver the keys and show the room, but there is no complaint. Thank you very much! Check-out at the front desk is fast. The door lock of the room is loose, the washbasin has a long crack, the bathroom door handle is off, the skirting is up, the carpet is old, and the guest room has not been repaired and maintained in time. The shower room has plenty of hot water and a large amount of water, making it very comfortable to take a bath. Rest at night is quite quiet. There are not many varieties of breakfast, which is quite satisfactory. It is convenient to take a taxi online when going out. There are only a few times when I go out, and there is only one service when I get on the car and close the door. Others basically do not see service personnel, and the door is very deserted. It is not far from Dinosaur Paradise and Wanda Plaza by car, and a little closer to Changzhou North Railway Station. The location is good. It is not easy for the hotel to persist until now. If it wants to continue to operate, necessary decoration and training are imperative.
